You would probably expect me to the be last person to say that Sendmail
is perfectly within their rights.  I have had a lot of problems with
what they are doing.

But what did you pay for Sendmail?  Was it a dollar, or was it more?
Let me guess.  It was much less than a dollar.  I bet you paid nothing.

So does anyone owe you anything, let alone a particular process which
you demand with such length?

Now, the same holds true with OpenSSH.  I'll tell you what.  If there is
ever a security problem (again :) in OpenSSH we will disclose it exactly
like we want, and in no other way, and quite frankly since noone has
ever paid a cent for it's development they have nothing they can say
about it.

Dear non-paying user -- please remember your place.

Or run something else.

OK?

Luckily within a few months you will be able to tell Sendmail how to
disclose their bugs because their next version is going to come out with
a much more commercial licence.  Then you can pay for it, and then you
can complain too.

Hi Ryan,
How are you? I will try to answer your questions as promptly as
possible. I don' t mind at all.


1. have you reported this to apple?  Have they acknowledged receiving
a report and said anything about a possible fix?

The short answer is no. Vendors are not interested in fixing issues
related to features in their products. Fixing it means removing it or
restricting it and that is not what they want.

It is quite interesting to be a security researcher today. You can see
patterns in the way various companies mitigate security problems found
in their products. I don't blame them. They are quite right from their
business point of you.

This is a quote from an article I wrote a month ago about disclosing
security vulnerabilities:

[quote]
For me and other people that I know, it is crucial to stay ahead of
the game. After all we are the good guys. It is not that we want to
satisfy our ego and that is the reason why we continue researching
these topics. All this research, could be valuable to professional
attackers but the tendency is that it will take some time until it
gets into mainstream exploitation. This gives us a couple of months
technological benefit that we will use for the good.

Now here is something that I learned from Mario Puzo's "The
Godfather". When the heads of all families gathered to discuss about
the potentials in the drug business there was only one of them that
made any sense. This dude, sorry I forgot his name, reasoned that
after all, although he don't believe in drugs, he will take part of
the business because then he can control it. As such he will do more
good than evil by not allowing drug lords to go to schools or other
public places.
[quote]

2. do you think this can be expanded in live attack scenarios? Can you
provide a few examples of what's maliciously possible?

Yes, IMHO this issue can be exploited on a massive scale. This is the
reason why I posted this security notice to full-disclosure and other
security related mailing lists.

Let's put it this way; media formats are the essence of today's
Internet. Youtube, Apple's Movie Trailers are just two of many other
websites that deals with media content.

iTunes and QuickTime are standard part of many business and home
workstations. QuickTime is widely spread technology in the business
sector due to its functionality. Also it is the default player in Mac
environments. Macs are getting quite popular today and this makes it
even worse.

Attackers can exploit the issues I found in many different ways with
various degree of success. This all depends on how skillful they are.
JavaScript and mainly browser related exploitation attacks are not as
mature as traditional buffer overflow attacks. It will take some time
for the bad guys to realise the potentials.

A skillful attacker can get complete access to the local filesystem
via this vulnerability. This effects all home users. In corporate
environments attackers are able to break into network devices and
hijack network interfaces and all this can be done through a simple
mp3, mp4, m4a, mov, avi, etc... file. You can see the potential
problems. Keep in mind that WEB traffic is usually allowed by many
firewall setups. This enables attackers to sneak into any network they
want totally unnoticed.

3. what triggered your interest in researching these backdoors?
understand you also worked closely on the pdf backdoor issue...

Yes, I participated in David's research although "Backdooring PDF" is
his own work. I am glad this issue was well covered by the media. We
were looking into backdooing PDF documents for quite a while and there
is a lot more to be said.

I have been researching client side security for quite a while. I
truly believe that this will be the next generation of attacks;
high-end hacking.

There are many other issue found in HTML, Flash, QuickTime files as
well. I welcome you to check my website. It is really hard for me to
summarize all issues in this correspondence. :)

4.  is this an implementation vulnerability?  Or just a feature that
can be manipulated maliciously?

It is quite useful feature actually. I guess it can be quite handy
when dealing with DVD content. Actually when I found this issue I
realised that I can use it to organize some media files I had hanging
around my home folder. It is quite handy feature.


5.  do you think we'll start seeing actual attacks using these
backdoors in popular file formats? Why?

Yes. You will see more of them I guarantee. I know for sure that this
issue can be used to create worms similar to Yamaner and Samy but with
much higher degree of impact. As I said earlier Word Documents, MP3s,
AVIs, MOVs can bypass firewalls and other network based protection
mechanisms. They can carry malicious payloads that upon execution will
bring attackers into your network.


6. lastly, is there a real name I can use?  Can you identify yourself?
Are you affiliated with a research company or working independently?

Well... my name is Petko D. Petkov. "pdp" is my initials. My other
nickname, "architect" was the result of a research I conducted years
ago based around passive hacking and information gathering attacks. A
lot of people started to reffer me as information architect since I
was dealing with quite a lot of information.

I am security research from UK. My research is independent while my
day work is based around non-standard penetration testing for various
companies in the London area.

If you have more questions please bash me an email.

Petko

do you know how to work with subversion ?... I recommend to download
the following IDE
http://www.aptana.com/, Install it with SVN support. It is called
Subclipse. Once you check a project out don't rush into commit. Just
make as many updates as possible. We don't have issue tracking system
so we need to synchronize via EMAIL. The goal for now is to write DOCS
and improve the DEMOS. I am fixing some libraries on AttackAPI core.
When you are checking out, concentrate on attackapi/branches/2.x .
This is what we are working on right now. When you are committing just
be as descriptive as possible because if both of us modify the same
file the next who commits need to merge the changes. Knowing what to
merge is good. Checkout once and if you think that the changes that
you made are enough for a commit just do it. The more commits you make
the more work for us because we have to merge every time. :)

And don't worry... this is SVN, so even if you get it wrong the
recovery is quite painless. Cool dude, we will chat latter :). I am
glad that you are joining me with this project. It will make my life
so much better :)

See you around

Date: Sat, 25 Nov 2006 02:03:31 +0000
From: "pdp (architect)" <pdp.gnucitizen@googlemail.com>
To: "Isaac Dawson" <isaac.dawson@gmail.com>
Subject: Re: [Dailydave] So when will the end of pen-tests begin?
Cc: Dailydave@lists.immunitysec.com
In-Reply-To: <5ff6321e0611222048v1940115cu249ce13d1f4ef1a1@mail.gmail.com>
MIME-Version: 1.0
Content-Type: text/plain; charset=ISO-8859-1; format=flowed
Content-Transfer-Encoding: 7bit
Content-Disposition: inline
References: <5ff6321e0611222048v1940115cu249ce13d1f4ef1a1@mail.gmail.com>
Delivered-To: pdp.gnucitizen@gmail.com

I don't think that pentesting will end at all. The approach will
change, that's for sure but people will always need help from the
security gods in order to protect themselves from the unknown. Sure,
the traditional pentesting approach will have less and less value in
the future. Today, in order to do a penetration test you don't need to
have any skills; just bunch of tools that you are already familiar
with it and that's it. Even web application testing, which in the past
used to be considered quite manual, can be automated today. However,
the customer is loosing the value of the service somewhere along the
line. It is good that penetration testing companies can generate 20
reports a day by empowering all the automated tools they have but how
valuable is that in a world where attackers are after this 0day or
that 0day. Attackers don't search for the ultimate solution any more.
They know that their trick will be discovered in the next 24 hours. So
in this time frame they have to do as much as possible. So,
penetration testers have to change in order to fit in this brave new
world.

IMHO, pentesting will go back to what it used to be at the beginning
and then flourish again. It is a loop. Everything well forgotten is
new.

On 11/23/06, Isaac Dawson <isaac.dawson@gmail.com> wrote:
> After reading Havlar's post on the 'end is near' of MSOffice bugs. It made
> me start thinking about when
> the end of pen-tests will begin. I don't know about the rest of you but I've
> seen huge differences in the types
>  of issues that are being found on thin/thick application pen tests.  Before
> it was very common to pretty much
> completely take control of servers. Although this does still happen, not
> nearly as much as before. Obviously
> this really depends on how mature the customers are and how many previous
> tests they've had.
>
> So when will these tests end? 5-10 years? 20? I know we will 'always' need
> security validation, but will customers
>  be willing to spend the (sometimes insanely overpriced) amount for these
> types of tests?
> Is anyone else thinking about what they will do next? :)
> -Isaac

here is the script you can use to create your own database

cheers mate

P.S. configure it appropriately

    s33 cr4p c0d3 b3l0w:

<?php
#
# CONFIG
#
$BUFFER_SIZE = 8192;
$CSVLINE_SIZE = 1000;

$DATABASE_USER = 'root';
$DATABASE_PASS = '';
$DATABASE_BASE = '';
$DATABASE_HOST = 'localhost';
$DATABASE_PREF = '';

if (is_file('config.php'))
	require_once 'config.php';

#
# INITIALIZE
#
if (!$DATABASE_USER || !$DATABASE_BASE || !$DATABASE_HOST)
	die('-- script not properly configured');

print("initialize datbase connection\n");

if (!($DB = mysql_connect($DATABASE_HOST, $DATABASE_USER, $DATABASE_PASS)))
	die('-- unable to initialize database connection');

print("initialize database base\n");

if (!(mysql_query("CREATE DATABASE IF NOT EXISTS $DATABASE_BASE", $DB)))
	die('-- failed to initialize base');

print("initialize database tables\n");

if (!(mysql_query("DROP TABLE IF EXISTS $DATABASE_BASE.__tmp_${DATABASE_PREF}
locations", $DB)))
	die('-- unable to drop temp table locations');

if (!(mysql_query("CREATE TABLE $DATABASE_BASE.__tmp_${DATABASE_PREF}locations (
	locId INT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
	country CHAR(2) NOT NULL,
	region CHAR(20) NOT NULL,
	city CHAR(20) NOT NULL,
	postalCode CHAR(10) NOT NULL,
	latitude CHAR(10) NOT NULL,
	longitude CHAR(10) NOT NULL,
	dmaCode INT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
	areaCode INT UNSIGNED NOT NULL)", $DB)))
	die('-- failed to initialize temp table locations');

if (!(mysql_query("DROP TABLE IF EXISTS $DATABASE_BASE.__tmp_${DATABASE_PREF}
blocks", $DB)))
	die('-- unable to drop temp table blocks');

if (!(mysql_query("CREATE TABLE $DATABASE_BASE.__tmp_${DATABASE_PREF}blocks (
	startIpNum INT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
	endIpNum INT UNSIGNED NOT NULL,
	locId INT UNSIGNED NOT NULL)", $DB)))
	die('-- failed to initialize temp table blocks');

#
# DOWNLOAD
#
print("retrieving geolitecity resource page\n");

if (!($contents = file_get_contents('http://www.maxmind.com/app/geolitecity')))
	die('-- unable to retrieve geolitecity resource page');

print("locating geolitecity resource\n");

if (!(preg_match('/<a href="(http:\/\/www.maxmind.com\/download\/geoip\/database
\/GeoLiteCity_CSV\/.*?\.zip)">/', $contents, $matches)))
	die('-- unable to locate geolitecity resource');

$geolitecity_resource = $matches[1];

print("locating geolitecity name\n");

if (!(preg_match('/.*\/(.*?)\.zip/', $geolitecity_resource, $matches)))
	die('-- unable to locate geolitecity name');

$geolitecity_resource_name = $matches[1];

if (!is_file($geolitecity_resource_name.'.zip')) {
	print("creating geolitecity database download location\n");

	if (!($fpout = fopen($geolitecity_resource_name.'.zip', 'wb')))
		die('-- unable to create geolitecity database download location');

	print("retriving geolitecity database");

	if (!($fpin = fopen($geolitecity_resource, 'r')))
		die('-- unable to retrive geolitecity database');

	while (!feof($fpin)) {
		$buffer = fread($fpin, $BUFFER_SIZE);
		fwrite($fpout, $buffer, $BUFFER_SIZE);
		echo '.';
	}

	fclose($fpout);
	fclose($fpin);

	print("\n");
}

#
# PROCESS LOCATIONS
#
print("opening geolitecity database locations\n");

if (!($fp = fopen('zip://'.dirname(__FILE__).'/'.$geolitecity_resource_name.'.zip#'.
$geolitecity_resource_name.'/GeoLiteCity-Location.csv', 'r')))
	die('-- unable to open geolitecity database locations');

print("processing geolitecity locations");

if (!(mysql_query("BEGIN", $DB)))
	die('-- unable to open transaction');

$index = 0;
$fields = null;
while (($row = fgetcsv($fp, $CSVLINE_SIZE)) !== false) {
	if (count($row) == 1)
		continue;

	if ($index++ == 0) {
		$fields = join(',', $row);
		continue;
	}

	$values = make_safe_values_string($row);

	$query = "INSERT INTO $DATABASE_BASE.__tmp_${DATABASE_PREF}locations ($fields)
    VALUES ($values)";

	if (!(mysql_query($query, $DB)))
		die("\n-- cannot import row; message: ".mysql_error($DB).'; index: '
        .$index.'; query: '.$query);

	echo '.';
}

if (!(mysql_query("COMMIT", $DB)))
	die('-- unable to commit transaction; message: '.mysql_error($DB));

fclose($fp);

print("\n");

#
# PROCESS BLOCKS
#
print("opening geolitecity database blocks\n");

if (!($fp = fopen('zip://'.dirname(__FILE__).'/'.$geolitecity_resource_name.'
.zip#'.$geolitecity_resource_name.'/GeoLiteCity-Blocks.csv', 'r')))
	die('-- unable to open geolitecity database blocks');

print("processing geolitecity blocks");

if (!(mysql_query("BEGIN", $DB)))
	die('-- unable to open transaction');

$index = 0;
$fields = null;
while (($row = fgetcsv($fp, $CSVLINE_SIZE)) !== false) {
	if (count($row) == 1)
		continue;

	if ($index++ == 0) {
		$fields = join(',', $row);
		continue;
	}

	$values = make_safe_values_string($row);

	$query = "INSERT INTO $DATABASE_BASE.__tmp_${DATABASE_PREF}blocks ($fields) 
    VALUES ($values)";

	if (!(mysql_query($query, $DB)))
		die("\n-- cannot import row; message: ".mysql_error($DB).'; index: '.
        $index.'; query: '.$query);

	echo '.';
}

if (!(mysql_query("COMMIT", $DB)))
	die('-- unable to commit transaction; message: '.mysql_error($DB));

fclose($fp);

print("\n");

#
# UPDATE DATABASES
#
print("update tables\n");

if (!(mysql_query("DROP TABLE $DATABASE_BASE.${DATABASE_PREF}locations", $DB)))
	die('-- unable to drop table locations');

if (!(mysql_query("RENAME TABLE $DATABASE_BASE.__tmp_${DATABASE_PREF}locations 
TO $DATABASE_BASE.${DATABASE_PREF}locations", $DB)))
	die('-- unable to update table locations');

if (!(mysql_query("DROP TABLE $DATABASE_BASE.${DATABASE_PREF}blocks", $DB)))
	die('-- unable to drop table locations');

if (!(mysql_query("RENAME TABLE $DATABASE_BASE.__tmp_${DATABASE_PREF}blocks TO 
$DATABASE_BASE.${DATABASE_PREF}blocks", $DB)))
	die('-- unable to update table blocks');

#
# HELPERS
#
function make_safe_values_string($array) {
	$tmp = array();

	foreach ($array as $item) {
		$tmp[] = "'".mysql_real_escape_string($item)."'";
	}

	return join(',', $tmp);
}

?>

drugo svruzano s hakerskiqt life style. v tozi sait se diktivat vschki
tendenci i osven tova edin den moze da bude chast ot produkciqta na
nqkoi film da rechem no tova se tvurde dalechni planove.

-- imam ideq da napravq sait prez koito companite shte mogat da nemira
experti i da gi naemat v grupi ili indivualno. vsichko taka,
zavisimost or rabotata koqto e svurshena the she mogat da ocenqvat
hakerite i po tozi nachin drugi companie shte mogat da si pravqt po
dobra seleciq.

-- imam ideq da napravq sait v koito hakerite shte sa chast ot social
network kudeto shte mogat da spodelqt dupkite v sigornosta koito
namirat, razgovarqt, discutirat, pishat blogove i izobshto vsichko
svurzano ot tqhniqt lifestyle.

Ot teb iskam da mi napravish strategiq kak tova vsichko moze da se
razvie. Da mi ismislih branding-a i da mi napravish communikacionata
campaniq. Iskam da mi izmislish imena ili da mi dadesh ideq za imena.
Iskam da se sreshtnesh s hora ot "the register" i drugi izdaniq s
koito da razgovarqsh za tezi proekti i s kakvo te doprinasqt.

V momenta v koito pochneme da iskarvame pari, ti garantiram da imash
50% ot vsichko samo za sebesi za da ne se chustvash zavisima ot men, i
tova ne e zashtoto ne sme dvoika... zashto sme i taka shte e v
budeshteto, no da budesh i da pravish tova koeto iskash. Az razbiram
kolko potiskasht e tvoq nachin na zivot i iskam da ti pomogna i da si
pomognem zaedno, nie dvamata.

Ako mi pomognesh sus vsichko tova milo, kato cqlo shte se chustvash po
dobre zashtoto:

* shte hodish navunka po chesto i shte se sreshtash s hora
* shte imash poveche neshta v portfolioto
* shte dobiesh poveche opit
* shte si chast ot neshto koeto go nqma
* shte imash vreme da si pravish toivte neshta i da si tursish rabota
kudeto si poiskash
* kogato si bremena nqma da se pretesnqvash dali shte imash rabota,
zashtoto shte imash

znam che malko napuvam no iskam da zapochna neshto da pravq do
sedmica, dve, inache  shte poludeiq... zashtoto glavata mi gumzi ot
idei. na purvo vreme iskam da ismilq imenata na drugite dva proekta.
